rakṣaṇīyaḥ prayatnāt ekasmin rakṣite jantau atra kāśau prayatnāt trailokya rakṣaṇāt puṇyam yat syāt tat syāt na saṃśayaḥ te eva rudrāḥ mantavyāḥ jīvanmuktāḥ na saṃśayaḥ te pūjyāḥ te namaskāryāḥ te santoṣyāḥ prayatnāt teṣu vai parituṣṭeṣu tuṣyet viśveśvaraḥ svayam yogakṣemaḥ vidhātavyaḥ teṣām viśveśituḥ mude kāśau vasanti ye martyāḥ dūra sthaiḥ api sat naraiḥ prasaraḥ tu indriyāṇām ca nivāryaḥ atra nivāsibhiḥ maraṇam na abhikāṅkṣet hi kākṣyaḥ mokṣaḥ api no punar śarīra śoṣaṇa upāyaḥ kartavyaḥ sudhiyā na hi śarīra sauṣṭhavam kāṅkṣyam vrata snāna ādi siddhaye bhātma rakṣā atra kartavyā mahā śreyas abhivṛddhaye madhu śarīra śoṣaṇa upāyaḥ kartavyaḥ na punar śarīra nāśāya iti arthaḥ hi na hi iti atra hetum āha śarīra sauṣṭhavam iti pāṭavam pauṣṭikam iti pāṭhe puṣṭi upāyam iti arthaḥ vinā ātmaghātam aśanam tyaktvā prāya upaveśanam anāśakam yaḥ kurute mad bhaktaḥ iha suvrataḥ mārga vārāṇasyām tat ekena prāṇāyāmena labhyate tat ānanda vane prāpyam maṇikarṇī eka majjanāt yat ṣoḍaśa mahā dānaiḥ puṇyam proktam mahā ṛṣibhiḥ tat puṇyam jāyate puṃsām viśveśe puṣpa dānāt tat pañca amṛtānām snapanāt viśveśe tat avāpyate sarva ṛtu kusuma āḍhyām ca yaḥ kuryāt puṣpa vāṭikām tad aṅgaṇe kalpavṛkṣāḥ chāyām kurvanti śītalām yaḥ kṣīra snapana artham vai viśveśe dhenum arpayet tasya nivaseyuḥ pitāmahāḥ yaḥ sudhām citram eva vā brāhmaṇān yatinaḥ vā api tathā eva śiva yoginaḥ bhojayet yaḥ atra vai kāśyām ekaika gaṇanā kramāt koṭi bhojya phalam tasya śraddhayā na atra saṃśayaḥ tat atra samavāpyate tat tat atra ānanda kānane japet yad yad yad yad phalam āpyate tasya puṇyam na jānāmi cintite ca akṣare pare tatra kāśau nityam pravastavyam sevya uttara vahā sadā āpadi api hi ghorāyām kāśī tyājyā na kutracid yatas sarva āpadām hartā trātā viśvapatiḥ prabhuḥ avandhyam divasam kuryāt snāna dāna japa ādibhiḥ prakﾱpate kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa ādīni kartavyāni prayatnāt kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa ādīni vyāsaḥ vakṣyati yāni vai teṣām svarūpam ākhyāhi skanda indriya viśuddhaye kathayāmi mahābuddhe kṛcchra ādīni te agratas yāni kṛtvā atra manujaḥ deha śuddhim labhet parām atha kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa karaṇa ādi anantaram na bādhante tad kartṛ narān iti arthaḥ upavāsena ca ekena pādakṛcchraḥ prakīrtitaḥ pratyekam pratyaham pītam parṇakṛcchraḥ prakīrtitaḥ piṇyāka ghṛta takra ambum saktūnām prativāsaram bhaikaikam upavāsaḥ ca kṛcchraḥ saumyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ haviṣā prātar aśnīta haviṣā sāyam eva ca haviṣā yācitam trīn tu sa upavāsaḥ tri aham vaset ekaikam grāsam aśnīyāt ahāni trīṇi pūrvavat payasā divasān ekaviṃśatiḥ dvādaśa aha upavāsena parākaḥ parikīrtitaḥ eka bhaktena ityādīnām padyānām ityādi sat pravṛttiḥ ca iti sārdha saptaviṃśatitama śloke anvayaḥ padmam piṇyākam tila piṣṭam ca ghṛtam ca taṅkram ca ambu ca saktuḥ ca teṣām pratyeka abhyavaharaṇam iti śeṣaḥ pūrvavat prātar ādi vat tri aham prātar tri aham sāyam tri aham adyāt a yācitam go mūtram gomayam kṣīram daghi sarpiḥ kuśa udakam eka rātra upavāsaḥ ca kṛcchraḥ sāṃtapanaḥ smṛtaḥ pṛthak sāntapana dravyaiḥ ṣaṣ ahar sa upavāsakaḥ tu kṛcchraḥ ayam mahāsāntapanaḥ smṛtaḥ taptakṛcchram caran vipraḥ jala kṣīra ghṛta anilān etān tri aham pibet uṣṇān sakṛt snāyī samāhitaḥ tri aham uṣṇāḥ pibet apaḥ tri aham uṣṇam payaḥ pibet tri aham uṣṇam ghṛtam prāśya vāyubhakṣaḥ dina trayam palam ekam payaḥ pītvā sarpiṣaḥ ca pala dvayam go mūtreṇa samāyuktam yāvakam yaḥ prayojayet kṛcchram eka āhnikam proktam śarīrasya viśodhanam hastau uttānatas kṛtvā divasam mārutāśanaḥ ekaikam hāsayet grāsam kṛṣṇe śukle ca vardhayet upaspṛśan triṣavaṇam etat cāndrāyaṇam smṛtam ekaikam vardhayet grāsam śukle kṛṣṇe ca hrāsayet bhuñjīta darśe no kiṃcid eṣa cāndrāyaṇaḥ vidhiḥ caturaḥ prātar aśnīyāt piṇḍān vipraḥ samāhitaḥ caturaḥ astam ite sūrye śiśucāndrāyaṇam smṛtam piṇḍān madhyaṃdine sthite niyata ātmā haviṣyasya yaticāndrāyaṇam smṛtam yathā kathaṃcid piṇḍānām tisraḥ aśītīḥ samāhitaḥ vidyā tapobhyām bhūta ātmā buddhiḥ jñānena śuddhi ati vyuṣṭaḥ prāpta prātar kālaḥ mahā cāndrāyaṇam brahmacāri cāndrāyaṇam tat ca jñānam bhavet puṃsām samyak kāśī niṣevaṇāt syāt viśveśa karuṇā udayaḥ tatas mahodayā avāptiḥ karma nirmūlana kṣamā atas kāśau prayatnena snānam dānam tapaḥ japaḥ mṛti ukta ādhya niṣevaṇam pratikṣaṇam pratidinam viśveśa pada cintanam liṅga arcanam tri kālam ca liṅgasya api pratiṣṭhitiḥ sādhubhiḥ saha saṃlāpaḥ jalpaḥ śivaiḥ śivaiḥ iti ca atitheḥ ca api satkāraḥ maitrī tīrtha nivāsibhiḥ hi a pratigraha vṛttiḥ ca matiḥ ca anugraha ātmakā ityādi sat pravṛttiḥ ca kartavyā kṣetra vāsinā nityam triṣavaṇa snāyī nityam bhikṣā kṛta aśanaḥ liṅga pūjā arcakaḥ nityam ittham vyāsaḥ vaset purā ekadā tasya jijñāsām kartum devīm haraḥ avadat adya bhikṣāṭanam prāpte vyāse parama dhārmike tathā iti uktvā bhavānī sā bhavam bhava nivāraṇam namaskṛtya pratigṛham tasya bhikṣām nyaṣedhayat sa muniḥ sahitaḥ śiṣyaiḥ bhikṣām a prāpya dūna vat ālokya punar babhrāma gṛhe gṛhe pariprāptā bhikṣā anyaiḥ sarva bhikṣukaiḥ tad ahninā alabhat bhikṣām sa śiṣyaḥ sa muniḥ kvacid atha sāyantanam karma kṛtvā chātraiḥ samanvitaḥ upoṣaṇa paraḥ bhūtvā tathā eva āsīt aharniśam atha anyedyus muniḥ vyāsaḥ kṛtvā mādhyāhnikam vidhim yayau bhikṣāṭanam kartum sa śiṣyaḥ paritas purīm bhikṣāṭanam prāpte bhikṣitum gate sati iti arthaḥ chattram iva gurum gopāyanti iti chātrāḥ śiṣyāḥ taiḥ ṣaṇṇavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ na kvāpi labdhavan bhikṣām bhāgya hīnaḥ dhanam yathā dvitrāḥ pavitra caraṇāt prāpya anujñām guroḥ atha samācakhyuḥ samāgamya dṛṣṭvā ṛdhim tat puraukasām śiṣyāḥ ūcuḥ śṛṇvantu ārādhya caraṇāḥ na upasargaḥ atra kaścana na anna kṣayaḥ vā sarvasyām nagaryām iha kutracid yatra viśveśvaraḥ sākṣāt yatra amara dhunī svayam tyādṛśāḥ yatra munayaḥ kva bhī tatra upasarga jā samṛddhiḥ yā gṛhasthānām iha viśveśituḥ puri yāvanti santi viśveśa nirmālya upabhujām gṛhe pavitra caraṇāt ārādhya caraṇāt viśveśa nirmālya laiṅgikānām devalakānām iti vā gṛhe gṛhe atra dhānyānām rāśayaḥ yādṛśaḥ punar na tādṛśaḥ kalpavṛkṣa dattāḥ aindre pure kvacid yatra sākṣāt viśāla akṣā su vistāra phala pradā nirvāṇa lakṣmyāḥ sadane tyasmin ānanda kānane sīmantinyaḥ striyaḥ sarvāḥ pati vrata parāyaṇāḥ sarvāḥ bhavānī rūpinyaḥ viśveśa arpita satkriyāḥ yāvantaḥ puruṣāḥ kāśyām sarve eva gaṇa adhipāḥ sarve eva kumārāḥ vai sarve tāraka dṛṣṭayaḥ tripuṇḍra aṅkita bhālāḥ ye te sarve candra maulayaḥ upasarga sahasraiḥ ca pīḍyamānāḥ api iha ye na tyajanti sadā kāśīm sarva jñāḥ eva te akhilāḥ gṛhe api brahma vāda vivādinaḥ yādṛśaḥ tādṛśaḥ iti ca bahuvacanam svardhunī dhūta kaluṣāḥ santi iha caturānanāḥ nirvāṇa lakṣmī patayaḥ kṣetra saṃnyāsa kāriṇaḥ sarve eva hṛṣīkeśāḥ sarve vai puruṣa uttamāḥ acyutāḥ eva vijñeyāḥ etad kṣetra parigrahāḥ striyaḥ vā puruṣāḥ vā api sarve eva na saṃśayaḥ śrīkaṇṭhāḥ sarve eva atra sarve mṛtyuṃjayāḥ dhruvam mokṣa śrī śrita varṣmāṇaḥ tu ardhanārīśvarāḥ yatas dharma rāśiḥ paraśvan atra mahantaḥ atra artha rāśayaḥ na garbha vāsa saṃsargaḥ kāśī saṃsthiti kāriṇām enāṃsi na atra bādhante viśveśa śaraṇa arthinaḥ yatra viśveśvaraḥ sākṣāt nāda bindu kalā ātmakaḥ sarasvatī sarit rūpā hi atas śāstra niketanam hi ānanda kānanam sarvam dharmaśāstra kṛta ālayam yāvantaḥ divi vai devāḥ tāvantaḥ atra mṛṣā na hi nīrājayanti viśveśam rātrau rātrau sadā ahayaḥ sva phaṇāmaṇi dīpaiḥ ca prāpya kāśīm rasātalāt samudrāḥ sarve eva atra kāmadhenu vraja anvitāḥ pañca pīyūṣa dhārābhiḥ viśveśam snapayanti hi mandāraḥ pārijātaḥ ca saṃtānaḥ haricandanaḥ nīrājayanti nīrājanām prāpayanti pañca pīyūṣa dhārābhiḥ pañcāmṛta sampātaiḥ yoginaḥ sarve sarve eva atra kāśīnātham upāsate vidyānām sadanam kāśī lakṣmyāḥ kāśī para ālayaḥ mukti kṣetram idam kāśā kāśā sarvā trayī mayā iti śrutvā muni varaḥ pārāśaryaḥ mahā tapāḥ evam babhāṣe tān śiṣyān punar ślokam paṭhantu amum ūcuḥ yānām ca āśrayaḥ kāśī kāśī lakṣyāḥ para ālayaḥ mukti kṣetram idam kāśā kāśā sarvā trayī mayā niśamya iti tadā vyāsaḥ krodha andhīkṛta locanaḥ bhū kṛśa anujcalat mūrtiḥ kāśīm śapsyati kumbhajaiḥ mā bhūtnaipūruṣī vidyā mā bhūtyaipūruṣam dhanam mā bhūt traipūruṣā muktiḥ kāśīm vyāsaḥ śapan iti iti kṛtvā matim vyāsaḥ kāśyām śāpam adāt tadā da tvā api śāpam saḥ muniḥ bhikṣitum krodhavān yayau babhrāma nagarīm sarvām kvā api bhaikṣam na labdhavan aṃśumālinam āvīkṣya manāk lohita maṇḍalam bhikṣā pātram parikṣipya niryayau āśramam prati atha gacchan mahādevyāḥ gṛha dvāri niṣaṇṇayā prākṛta strī svarūpinyāḥ bhikṣāyai prārthitaḥ atithiḥ bhagavan bhikṣukāḥ tāvat adya dṛṣṭāḥ na kutracid etādṛśa śāpe kāraṇam āha garvaḥ paraḥ atra vidyānām iti paraḥ hi atra vidyā iti pāṭhe niṣevate agham saḥ param sahitaḥ sva pitāmahaiḥ iti śrutvā gata a marṣaḥ vyāsaḥ tām āha vismitaḥ uvāca mahā sudhākarasya atha kuhū rāhu bhaya arditā sīmantinī sva rūpeṇa tiṣṭheḥ kāśyāma nirbhayā niśi saṃkocinam kāśyām vikāśinyām vaseḥ sadā kim vā nu karuṇā mūrtiḥ iha kāśi nivāsinām sarva duḥkha ogha hariṇī parā ānanda pradāyinī athavā kim vā nirvāṇa lakṣmī tvam yā kāśau parigīyate śvapākam yāyajūkam vā prānte alaṅkurvatī samam mad bhāgyam vā pariṇatam etat yoṣit svarūpāt athavā sā bhavet nūnam yā kṣetre parigīyate bhakta pota pradā bhaktyā bhavānī bhava nāśinī sarvathā eva na nārī tvam na āsurī na eva kinnarī na naḥ nāgā no gandharvī na yakṣiṇī tvam iṣṭadevatā eva asi kācid mama moha hāriṇī avaśyam eva kartā asmi te ādeśyam tat ādiśa ekam tapaḥ vyayam hitvā kārayiṣyasi yat punar tat eva aham kariṣyāmi vidheyaḥ śubha locane na vacaḥ tvādṛśāṇām hi mahā tvam hāpayet satām param tvam kā asi subhage satyam brūhi mama agratas iti pṛṣṭā āha muninā sā viśvāyuḥ ghaṭodbhavaiḥ ṣaṇṇavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ nityam vīkṣye carantam tvā bhikṣām śiṣya gaṇaiḥ vṛtam tvam eva mām naḥ jānīṣe jāne tvām aham eva hi prāṇa nāthasya me tāvat ātithyam saphalīkuru eka bhikṣām tadā aham tu kariṣye na anyathā punar tapasvī udīritam śrutvā sā provāca vacaḥ tatas aviśaṅkam vada mune kaḥ te asti niyamaḥ sudhīḥ iti śrutvā prahṛṣṭa ātmā saḥ tām āha tapodhanaḥ sudhīḥ iti kaṭākṣaḥ ayutam mama śiṣyāḥ ye taiḥ sa paktim aham vṛṇe niśamya iti prahṛṣṭa āsyā sā provāca munim tatas kim vilambena tat yāhi sarvān śiṣyān samāhvaya yena tṛptim gamiṣyanti mad śiṣyāḥ sarve eva te na māyātaḥ arthī yadā gehe siddham kāryam tadā eva hi paripūrṇāḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ paripūrṇāḥ manorathāḥ paripūrṇam gṛham sarvam pateḥ pāda prasādāt yāhi tūrṇam samāyāhi yāvat anna arthibhiḥ saha iti āśu gatvā samāgaccha yāvat na astamitaḥ raviḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ tvaritaḥ śiṣyān āhūya sarvatas āgatya tām punar prāha dṛṣṭvā tad mārga locanām mātar sarve samāyātāḥ tvaritam dehi bhojanam hi samayā samiyāt eṣa bhāskaraḥ tad maṇḍapa maṇi jyotiḥ tatyāhita dinaśriyaḥ katicid pariviṣṭa annāḥ bhoktum eva upaveśitāḥ tad mārga locanām vyāsa āgama vartma dṛṣṭim samīpe jyotis tati jyotis vistāra ādhā samarpay dina śrī yad tad svarjita svargam āśriyam iti pāṭhe saudha madhya viśeṣaṇam katicid pariviṣ anna pariviṣ annam yad tad yathā tad divya pāka sambhārān dṛṣṭvā tad dṛṣṭayaḥ kṣaṇāt parām tṛptim upāgacchan ghrāṇa nyāmoda rājibhiḥ atitṛptim samāpannāḥ te tad anna niṣevaṇāt mācāntāḥ candanaiḥ sragbhiḥ ambaraiḥ paribhūṣitāḥ atha sāṃdhyam vidhim kṛtvā propaviśya tad agratas tāvat vṛddha gṛhasthena gṛhiṇī sā kaṭākṣitā uvāca svaccha antaḥkaraṇe mātar mahā miṣṭānna mānade tvam eva dharmam jānāsi pati śuśrūṣaṇe ratā yadi pṛcchasi mām satyam tadā kiṃcana vacmi te vaktavyam eva pṛṣṭena manāk api vijānatā yena eṣa toṣam āyāti tava bhartā cirantanaḥ sādhāraṇāni dharmāṇi sampṛcche tāni me vada uvāca anudvega karam vākyam para utkarṣa sahiṣṇu tā miṣṭhā annam ca mānaḥ ca iti dvaṃdvaḥ uvāca tad dānta tā tava eva aikṣi dānam śāpasya ca uttamam tvayi eva samyak dṛśyeta para utkarṣa sahiṣṇu tā vicārya kāritāyāḥ ca tvam eva nilayaḥ mahān mama ekam brūhi bho vidvas śāpam dadyāt ca yaḥ krudhā uvāca uvāca bhavatā bhramatā vipraiḥ na āptā bhikṣā yadā api aho tadā aparāddham kim iha varākaiḥ kṣetra vāsibhiḥ tapasvin śṛṇu mama vākyam rājadhānyām mama iha yaḥ mṛddhim draṣṭum na śaknoti pariśaptaḥ saḥ eva hi tvadvidhānām na yogyam mama kṣetram mokṣa eka sādhanam atra a alpam api yat daṣṭyam kṛtam mad kṣetra vāsinām tad dauṣṭyasya parīpākaḥ rudra paiśācyam eva hi tat śrutvā vepamānaḥ sa pariśuṣka oṣṭha tālukaḥ jagāma śaraṇam gaurīm luṭhan tad caraṇa agratas uvāca ca vacaḥ mātar trāhi trāhi bhṛśam rudn anāthaḥ tvad sanāthaḥ aham bāliśaḥ te bālakaḥ ca saṃtrāhi rakṣa mām śaraṇa āgatam bahūnām āgasām geham mama duṣṭa mānasam śambhu śāpaḥ anyathā kartum bhavatyā api na śakyate mama ca śaraṇa āyātaḥ tat ekam kriyatām śive pratyaṣṭame sadā kṣetre pratibhūtam ca pārvati diśa praveśana ādeśam na īśaḥ tvad vākya laṅghakaḥ iti uktā tena muninā bhavānī karuṇā janiḥ mukham maheśituḥ vīkṣya tathā iti āha tad ājñayā vyāsaḥ api niryayau kṣetrāt sva aparādha vaśam vadan ahar rātram sa paśyan vai kṣetram dṛṣṭyāḥ adūra gam prāpya aṣṭamām ca bhūtām ca madhyekṣetram sadā viśet sthitaḥ hi adya api paśyet saḥ kāśi prāsāda rājikām svaḥ ca asau aparādha vaśaḥ ca tam ātmānam vadati iti tathā chāndasaḥ luk abhāvaḥ ittham kumbhaja sa vyāsaḥ kṣetre śāpam pradāsyati kṣetra śāpa pradānāt ca bahis yāsyati tad kṣaṇāt atas eva avimuktasya kṣetrasya śubha śaṃsinaḥ śrutvā adhyāyam imam puṇyam vyāsa śāpa vimokṣaṇam iti śrī skandapurāṇe kāśīkhaṇḍe vyāsaśāpavimokṣaṇam nāma ṣaṇṇavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ iti śrī rāmānanda kṛtāyām kāśīkhaṇḍa ṭīkāyām ṣaṇṇavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ etat bhaviṣyam śrutvā aham vyāsasya śiva nandanaiḥ māścarya bhājanam jātaḥ tīrthāni kathaya adhunā parama ānanda kānane yāni yatra santi ṣaḍānana tāni liṅga svarūpāṇi samācakṣva mama agratas yādṛśaḥ kathitaḥ vacmi tādṛśam śṛṇu kumbhajaiḥ tāni tāni iha mama kāśau tatra tatra vada prabho śṛṇu devi viśāla akṣe tīrtham liṅgam udāhṛtam parigrahāt tīrthānām kriyate sarva pāpa he viśāla akṣe tarhi jalāśaya ādeḥ katham tīrtha tvam tatra āha iti mūrtayaḥ brahma viṣṇu arka śiva vighneśvara ādikāḥ mahādevaḥ prathamam tīrtham ucyate kṣetra pūrvottare bhāge tat dṛṣṭam paśu pāśa hṛt tad paścāt vigrahavatī pūjyā vārāṇasī naraiḥ mahādevasya pūrveṇa goprekṣam liṅgam uttamam go lokāt preṣitāḥ gāvaḥ pūrvam yat śambhunā svayam mūrti rūpam liṅgam iti anvayaḥ paśavaḥ jīvāḥ teṣām pāśāḥ caturviṃśati tattvāni tad hṛt samāyātāḥ tad darśanāt bhavet puṃsām phalam yajña samudbhavam tu tavyācyām madhu kaiṭabha pūjitam liṅgam dṛṣṭvā prayatnena vaiṣṇavam padam ṛcchati tasya sampūjanāt martyaḥ vijvaraḥ jāyate kṣaṇāt tu kṣetrajñaḥ ca ādikeśavaḥ dṛṣṭam tribhuvanam sarvam tasya saṃdarśanāt dhruvam saṃgameśvaram ālokya tavyācyām jāyate anaghaḥ tatra śāntikarī gaurī pūjitā śānti kṛt bhavet paraḥ kṣetrajñaḥ īśvaraḥ vidhinā sthāpitam iti śeṣaḥ varaṇāyāḥ taṭe pūrve pūjyam kuntīśvaram nṛbhiḥ tad pūjanāt prajāyante putrāḥ nija kula ujjcalāḥ kuntīśvarāt uttaratas tīrtham vai kāpilaḥ hṛdaḥ tatra vai snāna mātreṇa vṛṣabhadhvaja pūjanāt tatra śrāddhe kṛte putraiḥ pitṛ lokam prayānti te mune tad darśanāt bhavet strīṇām pātivratya phalam sphuṭam tad liṅga pūrva digbhāge pūjyaḥ siddhi vināyakaḥ yām siddhim yaḥ samīheta saḥ tām āpnoti tad natyāḥ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ liṅgam gaṇeśāt paścime tatas sthāpitam kumbhīśvaram iti kvacid raurava ādiṣu ādi śabdena mahāraurava ādayaḥ gṛhyante yām siddhim abhīṣṭām siddhim tad natyāḥ tasya namaskārāt hiraṇyakūpaḥ tatra asti hiraṇya aśva samṛddhi kṛt muṇḍāsureśvaram liṅgam tat pratīcyām ca siddhi dam tu nairṛtyām goprekṣāt vṛṣabheśvaram mune skandeśvaram liṅgam mahādevasya paścime tad liṅga pūjanāt nṛṇām bhavet mama salokatā tad pārśvatas hi śākheśaḥ viśākheśaḥ ca tatra vai teṣām api hi liṅgāni tatra santi sahasraśas tad darśanāt bhavet puṃsām tad tad gaṇa salokatā ca śilādeśaḥ kudhīharaḥ mahā bala pradaḥ tatra hiraṇyākṣeśvaraḥ śubhaḥ tad dakṣiṇe aṭṭahāsa ākhyam liṅga sarva sukha pradam tad uttare prasanna udam kuṇḍam nairmalya dam nṛṇām pratīcyām aṭṭahāsasya mitrāvaruṇa nāmnī liṅge tad loka de pūjye mahāpātaka hāriṇī naiṛtyām ca aṭṭahāsasya vṛddhavāsiṣṭha saṃjñakam liṅgam tad pūjanāt puṃsām jñānam utpadyate mahat vasiṣṭha īśa samīpa sthaḥ kṛṣṇa īśaḥ viṣṇu loka daḥ tad yāmyām yājñavalkya īśaḥ brahma tejas vivardhanaḥ svayam līnaḥ śivaḥ yatra bhakta anugraha kāmyayā atas sva līnam tad pūrve liṅgam pūjyam prayatnāt sadā eva jñāna niṣṭhānām paramānandam icchatām yā gatiḥ vihitā teṣām sva līne sā tanutyajām vairocaneśvaram liṅgam svalīnāt puratas sthitam tatra eva liṅgam bāṇeśam pūjitam sarva kāma dam candreśvarasya pūrveṇa liṅgam vidyeśvara abhidham tad dakṣiṇe tu vīreśaḥ mahā siddhi vidhāyakaḥ pañcamudram mahāpīṭham tat jñeyam sarva siddhi dam tatra japtāḥ mahā mantrāḥ kṣipram siddhyanti na a anyathā tad pīṭhe vāyu koṇe tu sampūjyaḥ sagara īśvaraḥ tad īśāne ca vālīśaḥ tiryagyoni nivārakaḥ mahā pāpa ogha vidhvaṃsī sugrīva īśaḥ tad uttare māśvineya īśvarau pūjyau gaṅgāyāḥ paścime taṭe tad uttare bhadrahṛdaḥ gavām kṣīreṇa pūritaḥ pūrvābhādrapada yuktā paurṇamāsī yadā bhavet tadā puṇyatamaḥ kālaḥ vājimedha phala pradaḥ go lokam prāpnuyāt tasmāt puṇyāt na eva atra saṃśayaḥ bhadreśvarāt yātudhānyām upaśānta śivaḥ mune tasya liṅgasya saṃsparśāt parām śāntim samṛcchati upaśānta śivam liṅgam dṛṣṭvā janma śata arjitam tyajet aśreyasoḥ rāśim śreyas rāśim ca vindati māśvineya īśvarau aśvinī kumārābhyām sthāpitau nairṛtyām mahā lokam avāpnoti bhāvitena antarātmanā tat nairṛte ca śūla īśaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ ca prayatnāt śūlam tatra purā nyastam snāna artham varavarṇini hṛdaḥ tatra samutpannaḥ śūla īśasya agratas mahān snānam kṛtvā hade tatra dṛṣṭvā śūleśvaram vibhum liṅgam ca sthāpitam śreṣṭham kuṇḍam ca api śubham kṛtam tatra kuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā vai nāradeśvaram saṃsāra abdhim mahā ghoram santaret na a tra saṃśayaḥ tad agre tāmrakuṇḍam ca tatra snātaḥ na garbha bhāj vighna hartā gaṇādhyakṣaḥ tad vāyavye gaṇādhyakṣaḥ tad vāyavye su vighna hṛt tat udañc diśi ca uttamam yat kuṇḍam ca anāraka ākhyam vai tatra snātaḥ na nārakī varaṇāyāḥ taṭe ramye varaṇeśaḥ tad uttare tatra pāśupataḥ siddhaḥ tu akṣapādaḥ mahā mune anena eva śarīreṇa śāśvatām siddhim āgataḥ tad paścime ca śaileśaḥ para nirvāṇa kāma daḥ tu tat yāmyām liṅgam śāśvata siddhi dam koṭitīrthe hade snātvā koṭīśam paripūjya ca gavām koṭi pradānasya phalam āpnoti mānavaḥ mahāśmaśāna stambhaḥ asti koṭīśāt vahni diś sthitaḥ tatra eva tīrtham paramam kapāleśa samīpatas pālamocanam nāma tatra snātaḥ aśvamedha bhāj tu tad udañc diśi śobhanam tatra eva aṅgārakam tīrtham kuṇḍam kuṇḍam ca aṅgāranirmalam snātvā aṅgārakatīrthe tu bhavet bhūyas na garbha bhāj aṅgāravāra yuktāyām caturthyām snāti yaḥ naraḥ na abhibhūyeta na ca duḥkhī kadācana viśvakarma īśvaram liṅgam jñāna dam ca tad uttare mahāmuṇḍeśvaram liṅgam tasya dakṣiṇatas śubham śmaśāna vat ati bhīṣaṇa tvāt śmaśāna stambhaḥ kula stambhaḥ iti prasiddhaḥ bhavati ca bhavati eva ṛṇāt ṛṇa trayāt aṅgāra nirmalam jvalat aṅgāra vat ujjvalam niścitam tatra muṇḍa mayā mālā mayā kṣiptā ati śobhanā mahāmuṇḍā tatas devī samutpannā agha hāriṇī khaṭvāṅgam ca dhṛtam tatra khaṭvāṅga īśaḥ tatas abhavat niṣpāpaḥ jāyate martyaḥ bhuvaneśaḥ tatas yāmyām kuṇḍam ca bhuvaneśvaram tatra kuṇḍe naraḥ snātaḥ bhuvaneśaḥ bhavet naraḥ tad yāmyām vimaleśaḥ ca kuṇḍam ca vimalodakam tatra snātvā vilokya īśam vimalaḥ jāyate naraḥ tatra pāśupataḥ siddhaḥ tryambakaḥ nāma nāmnaḥ bhṛgoḥ āyatanam tasya paścime atīva puṇya dam mahā śubha phala pradaḥ tatra siddhaḥ pāśupataḥ kapila ṛṣiḥ mahā tapāḥ oṃkāraḥ eṣaḥ eva asau ādi varṇa maya ātmakaḥ na ādeśaḥ paramam brahma na ādeśaḥ paramā gatiḥ na ādeśaḥ paramam sthānam duḥkha saṃsāra mocanam matsyodarī sā kathitā snānam puṇyaiḥ avāpyate matsyodarī yadā gaṅgā paścime kapileśvaram samāyāti mahādevi tadā yogaḥ su durlabhaḥ uddālakeśvaram liṅgam udīcyām kapileśvarāt paścime tasyāḥ paścime tad uttare bāṣkulīśam liṅgam sarva artha siddhi dam tat bāṣkulīśāt dakṣiṇatas liṅgam vai kaustubheśvaram maṅkukarṇeśvaram liṅgam kaustubheśvara dakṣiṇe saṃsevya paramam jñānam labhet adya api sādhakaḥ tat tat tat tat tat tat uttare śubhaḥ tatra tad liṅgayoḥ samarcāyāḥ siddhiḥ bhavati vāñchitā tad dakṣiṇe mahā kuṇḍam rudrāvāsaḥ iti smṛtam caturdaśī yadā aparṇe rudra nakṣatra saṃyutā tadā puṇyatamaḥ kālaḥ tasmin kuṇḍe mahā phalaḥ rudrakuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā rudreśvaram vibhum tad agre pitṛkūpaḥ asti pitṝṇām ālayaḥ paraḥ tatra śrāddham naraḥ kṛtvā piṇḍān kūpe parikṣipet ekaviṃśa kula upetaḥ śrāddha kṛt rudra loka bhāj tatra vaitaraṇī nāma dīrghikā paścima ānanā bṛhaspatīśvaram liṅgam rudrakuṇḍāt ca paścime guru puṣya samāyoge dṛṣṭvā divyām labhet giram rudra āvāsāt dakṣiṇatas kāmeśam liṅgam uttamam tad dakṣiṇe mahā kuṇḍam snānāt cintita kāma dam rudra nakṣatram ārdrā caitra śukla trayodaśyām tatra yātrā ca kāma dā nalakūbara liṅgam ca prācyām kāmeśvarāt śubham tad agre pāvanaḥ kūpaḥ dhana dhānya samṛddhi daḥ malakūbara pūrveṇa sūryācandramasā īśvarau ajñāna dhvānta paṭalām harataḥ tau samarcitau tad dakṣiṇe adhva keśaḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ moha vināśanaḥ tatra eva maṇḍala īśaḥ ca maṇḍala īśa pada pradaḥ kāmakuṇḍasya pūrveṇa cyavaneśaḥ samṛddhi daḥ tad yāmyām āhutīśaḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ homa phala pradaḥ tad yāmyām puṇya janakam liṅgam pañcaśikha īśvaram tasmin hrade naraḥ snātvā kim bhūyas pariśocati tatra snānam ca dānam ca bhavet akṣaya puṇya dam dīkṣām pāśupatām labdhvā dvādaśa abdena yat phalam tat phalam labhate vipraiḥ martyaḥ kuṇḍeśa darśanāt mārkaṇḍeya hradāt pūrvam śāṇḍilya īśaḥ su puṇya daḥ tad paścime ca caṇḍeśaḥ caṇḍāṃśu grahaṇa agha hṛt dakṣiṇe ca kapāla īśāt kuṇḍam śrīkaṇṭha saṃjñitam tatra kuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā dātā syāt śrī prabhāvāt mahālakṣmīśvaram liṅgam tasya kuṇḍasya saṃnidhau mahā lakṣmīm samabhyarcya snātaḥ tad kuṇḍa vāriṣu tadā tena eva mārgeṇa yānti strībhiḥ vṛtāḥ sukham caṇḍāṃśugrahaṇā agha hṛt caṇḍāṃśugrahaṇam yāvat agham harati tāvat agha hṛt tad kuṇḍa dakṣiṇe bhāge liṅgam brahma pada pradam gāyatrī īśvara sāvitrī īśvarau pūjyau prayatnāt tayoḥ pūrveṇa sampūjyam tapaḥ śrī parivardhanam ugreśvaram mahā liṅgam lakṣmīśāt pūrva diś sthitam tad dakṣiṇe ca ugra kuṇḍam snānāt kanakhala adhikam karavīreśvaram liṅgam tasya kuṇḍasya paścime tasya darśanāt puṃsām jāyate roga saṃkṣayaḥ tat vāyavye marīci īśam kuṇḍam ca agha ogha nāśanam tad paścāt ca aindra kuṇḍam ca liṅgam ca indreśvaram mune pūrve tat kanakhalam haridvāram gayā vā antara tīrtha viśeṣaḥ vā tatra vāpī jale snātvā dṛṣṭvā karkoṭakeśvaram nāgānām ādhipatyam tu jāyate na atra saṃśayaḥ tad paścāt damicaṇḍa īśaḥ brahmahatyā haraḥ haraḥ tad dakṣiṇe mahā kuṇḍam rudra loka phala pradam tad paścime mahā liṅgam agnīśaḥ iti viśrutam āgneyam nāma kuṇḍam ca tat pūrve agni salokata dam māgneya īśvarataḥ prācyām kuṇḍam tad dakṣiṇe śubham tatra kuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā svarge vasati pūrvajaiḥ tad prācyām bālacandreśaḥ candraloka gati pradaḥ paritas bālacandra īśam gaṇa liṅgāni anekaśas labhet bālacandra samīpe tu kūpaḥ pitṛ gaṇa priyaḥ tatra śrāddha pradaḥ snātvā pitṝn sapta atra tārayet hi puṇḍam iti śeṣaḥ tat andhoḥ pūrvatas liṅgam puṇyam viśveśvara āhvayam haraḥ yaiḥ tu tatra udakam pītam strībhiḥ puṃbhiḥ sva karmabhiḥ tatra kūpe tu yat dattam dānam śiva rata ātmanām saṃvarte api na tasya asti nāśaḥ kalaśasambhavaiḥ khaṇḍa sphuṭita saṃskāram tatra kurvanti ye narāḥ mṛd tu īśaḥ tu apamṛtyu hṛt liṅgam dakṣeśvara āhvam ca tatas kūpāt udañc diśi mahākāla īśa liṅgam ca dakṣeśāt pūrvatas mahat mahākuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā mahākālam tu yaḥ arcayet tad yāmyām na antakasya bhī hastipāleśvaram liṅga tasya dakṣiṇatas mune tatra airābata kuṇḍam ca liṅgam airāvateśvaram tad dakṣiṇe śreyase ca liṅgam syāt mālatīśvaram bandīśvaraḥ mahākālakuṇḍāt uttaratas śubhaḥ bandikuṇḍam ca vikhyātam vārāṇasyām mahā agha hṛt mahākālakuṇḍe tatra snānena dānena śrāddhena akṣayam aśnute hi dhanvantari īśvaram liṅgam kuṇḍam tad nām ca eva hi tasya liṅgasya nām anyat kuṇḍa nām anyat eva hi tuṅgeśvaram liṅga nāma kuṇḍam vaidyeśvara abhidham sudhā mayyaḥ mahā auṣadhyaḥ kṣiptāḥ tatra mahā dhiyaḥ tad kuṇḍa snānāt tasmāt tad liṅga parivīkṣaṇāt naśyanti vyādhayaḥ sarve saha pāpaiḥ su dāruṇaiḥ tad uttare halīśa īśaḥ sarva vyādhi niṣūdanaḥ tuṅga nāmnaḥ ca dakṣiṇe jamadagnīśvaram liṅgam śiva īśāt dakṣiṇe śubham iti sudhā mayyaḥ yāḥ mahauṣadhyaḥ mṛtasañjīvinī ādi rūpāḥ vartante tāḥ mahā mahauṣadhyaḥ tatra tat nairṛtyām ca vyāsa īśaḥ kūpaḥ ca vimala udakaḥ vyāsakūpe naraḥ snātvā tarpayitvā surān pitṝn akṣayam labhate lokam yatra kutra abhikāṅkṣitam ghaṇṭākarṇa hṛde snātvā vyāsa īśa paridarśanāt yatra tatra mṛtaḥ vā api vārāṇasyām mṛtaḥ bhavet pañcacūḍā jale snātvā dṛṣṭvā devam tam īśvaram svarga lokam naraḥ yāti pañcacūḍā priyaḥ bhavet pañcacūḍa uttare bhāge tīrtham ca aśoka saṃjñitam mandākinī mahā tīrtham tat udīcyām mahā agha hṛt tam īśvaram pañcacūḍa īśam iti arthaḥ tatra jāgaraṇam kṛtvā aśoka aṣṭamyām madhau naraḥ mukti kṣetra pramāṇam ca krośam krośam ca sarvatas madhyameśvarāt etat eva sadā prāhuḥ sarve vai prapitāmahāḥ kaścid mad kule jātaḥ mandākinyāḥ jala āplutaḥ bhojayet prayataḥ viprān yatīn pāśupatān api mandākinyām naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā vai madhyameśvaram madhyameśādavācyām ca viśvedeva īśvaraḥ śubhaḥ tad arcanāt arcitāḥ syuḥ viśvedevāḥ trayodaśa tad pūrve vīrabhadra īśa om mahāvīra pada pradaḥ bhadradā bhadrakālī ca tasya dakṣiṇatas śubhā bhadrakālahadaḥ nāma tatra atīva śubha pradaḥ hi hrada paścimatas liṅgam śaunakeśam sudhī pradam tatra naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā vai śaunaka īśvaram tat saṃlabhet divyam yena mṛtyum tarati asau mataṃgeśasya vāyavye nānā liṅgāni sarvatas brahmarāteśvaram liṅgam mataṃga īśāt ca dakṣiṇe tatra ājyapeśvaram liṅgam pitṛ liṅgāni anekaśas tad liṅga sevayā sarve tuṣyanti prapitāmahāḥ tad dakṣiṇe siddha kūpaḥ siddhāḥ santi sahasraśas bāyu rūpāḥ tu ye siddhāḥ ye siddhāḥ bhānu raśmi gāḥ taiḥ sthāpitam tu yat liṅgam tat siddheśvaram īritam tasya saṃdarśanāt eva sarvāḥ syuḥ siddhayaḥ amalāḥ tad paścime siddha vāpī pītā snātā ca siddhi dā prācyām ca siddha kūpāt vai liṅgam vyāghreśvarā abhidham tad liṅga darśanāt nṛṇām na bhayam vyāghra cora jam ca tad dakṣiṇe mudām dhām liṅgam prahasita īśvaram tad uttare nivāsa īśaḥ kāśi vāsa phala pradaḥ xchā devī tu tatra asti natā jyeṣṭha pada pradā avācyām vyāghraliṅgāt ca liṅgam caṇḍīśvarā abhidham tad uttare daṇḍakhātam saraḥ pitṛ mudā āvaham ha iṣavya guhā tatra tatra liṅgam tad āhvayam mahā puṇya pradam liṅga tat paścāt devaleśvaram śatakālaḥ tad samīpe śatam kālān umāpatiḥ tad liṅga āvirbhave kāśau kālayāmāsa kumbhajaiḥ tad liṅga darśanāt āyuḥ śata varṣāṇi akhaṇḍitam mahā japa phala pradaḥ tad dakṣiṇe kṣapā deśaḥ mahājñāna pravartakaḥ tad agre ca kaṇā deśaḥ tatra puṇya udakaḥ prahiḥ snātvā kāṇādakūpe yaḥ kaṇādeśam samarcayet tasya dakṣiṇatas dṛśyaḥ bhūtīśaḥ bhūti kṛt satām tad paścime agha saṃhartṛ āṣāḍhīśvara saṃjñitam durvāsa īśaḥ ca tad pūrve sarva kāma samṛddhi kṛt tad yāmyām bhāra bhūta īśaḥ pāpa bhāra apahārakaḥ vyāseśvarasya pūrveṇa dvau śaṅkha likhiteśvarau tau dṛśyau yatnatas kāśau mahājñāna pravartakau yat samāpya āpyate puṇyam niṣṭhā pāśupata vratam tat āpyate atra viśveśa sakṛt īkṣaṇāt kṣaṇāt akṣapāda iti chedaḥ kūpaḥ durvāsa īśaḥ kāmeśāt tena sthāpitāt anyaḥ ārṣaḥ durvāsaḥ vā kaścid tad īśāne avadhūta īśaḥ yoga jñāna pravartakaḥ tīrtham ca eva avadhūteśam sarva kalmaṣa nāśa kṛt avadhūteśvarāt pūrve liṅgam paśupatīśvaram tad liṅga sevayā puṃsām paśu pāśa vimokṣaṇam tad dakṣiṇe gobhila īśaḥ mahā abhilaṣita pradaḥ xc mayūkha arkaḥ pañcanade gabhasti īśaḥ ca tatra vai dadhikalpahadaḥ nāma tad udīcyām mahā prahiḥ durlabham te yahi snānam durlabham ca tad īkṣaṇam naraḥ tam āśu saṃvīkṣya kalpam tryakṣa pure vaset uddiśya maṅgalām gaurīm bhojayet vija dampatī alaṅkṛtya yathāśakti tad puṇya antaḥ na karhicit pradakṣiṇa phalā maṅgala ekā pradakṣiṇā vadanaprekṣaṇādevī mukhaprekṣā īśvarā uttare maṅgalāyāḥ samīpe tu sarva siddhi karā śivā liṅge tvaṣṭṛ īśa vṛtta īśau mukha prekṣā uttare śubhe tad uttare carcikāyāḥ devyāḥ sandarśanam śubham revateśvara liṅgam ca carcikā agreṇa śānti kṛt mahā śubhāya tasya agre liṅga pañcanada īśvaram maṅgalodaḥ mahā kūpaḥ maṅgalā paścime śubhaḥ upamanyoḥ mahā liṅgam maṅgalā paścime śubham vyāghrapādeśvaram liṅgam tad paścāt vyāghrabhītihṛt nairṛtyām ca gabhastīśāt śaśāṅka īśaḥ agha saṃgha hṛt revata īśāt paścimatas jaimini īśaḥ mahā agha hṛt tatra liṅgāni anekāni ṛṣīṇām ṛṣi sattamaiḥ jaimineśāt ca vāyavye liṅgam vai rāvaṇeśvaram na tad darśanāt puṃsām rākṣasāṇām mahā bhayam tad dakṣiṇe varāha īśaḥ varāha īśaḥ māṇḍavya īśaḥ tatas yame tad dakṣiṇe pracaṇḍeśaḥ yogeśaḥ dakṣiṇe tatas tad dakṣiṇe ca dhātā īśaḥ soma īśaḥ ca tad agratas tat nairṛtyām kanakeśaḥ mahā kanaka daḥ satām tad uttare pāṇḍavānām pañca liṅgāni sat mude tad paścāt kalaśa īśaḥ ca liṅgam kālāḥ abhaya pradam citragupteśvaram liṅgam tat udīcyām agha apaham citragupteśvarāt paścāt yaḥ dṛḍheśaḥ mahā phalaḥ halaśa īśāt avācyām ca graha īśaḥ liṅgam uttamam citragupta īśvarāt paścāt yadṛcchā īśaḥ mahā phalaḥ tathya vāmadeva īśam liṅgam yāmyām graheśvarāt ca tasya dakṣiṇatas śubhe tad yāmyām maṇikarṇīśam tad udañc paliteśvaram jarā haram ca tatra eva tat paścāt pāpa nāśanam tat yābhyām nirjara īśaḥ tat nairṛtyām pitāmahaḥ pitāmahasrotikā ca tatra śrāddham mahā phalam tad yāmyām varuṇeśaḥ ca bāṇeśaḥ tasya dakṣiṇe kūṣmāṇḍa īśaḥ tu siddhikṛt tad pūrvatas rākṣasa īśaḥ gaṅgeśaḥ tasya dakṣiṇe tad uttare nimnagā īśāḥ santi liṅgāni anekaśas jarā haram liṅgam iti śeṣaḥ tad paścāt aditīśaḥ ca cakreśaḥ tasya ca agratas tad agre kālakeśa ākhyaḥ dṛṣṭa pratyaya kṛt paraḥ chāyā saṃdṛśyate tatra niṣpāpaḥ tad avekṣaṇāt tad agre tārakeśaḥ ca tad agre svarṇa bhāra daḥ tad uttare marutta īśaḥ śakra īśaḥ ca tad agratas tad dakṣiṇe ca rambheśaḥ tatra eva ca śaśīśvaraḥ tad uttare lokapa īśāḥ tatra liṅgāni anekaśas nāga gandharva yakṣāṇām kiṃnara apsarasām api deva ṛṣi gaṇa vṛndānām nānā siddhi karāṇi api śakreśāt dakṣiṇe bhāge phālguna īśaḥ mahā agha hṛt mahāpāśupata īśaḥ ca tad yāmyām śubha kṛt paraḥ tad paścime samudreśaḥ īśāna īśaḥ tad uttare tad pūrve lāṅgalī īśaḥ ca sarva siddhi samarpakaḥ rāga dveṣa vinirmuktāḥ siddhim yānti ca pūjakāḥ teṣām mokṣaḥ mayā ākhyātaḥ na tu te devi mānavāḥ madhupiṅga śvetaketū lāṅgalīśe ca tapasvinaḥ ekam jāgaraṇam kṛtvā prītikeśaḥ upoṣitaḥ devasya dakṣiṇe bhāge tatra vāpī śubha udakā tat ambuprāśanam nṝṇām apunarbhava hetave tad jalāt paścime bhāge daṇḍapāṇiḥ sadā avati tad prācī avācī uttarāyām tāraḥ kālaḥ śilāda jaḥ śivarātrau yaiḥ tatra tat jalam pītam kṛtārthāḥ te nara uttamāḥ tad udīcyām samarcayet svarṇākṣa īśaḥ tu tavyācyām jñānadaḥ tasya ca uttare viśveśāt dakṣiṇe bhāge nikumbha īśaḥ prayatnāt tad kṣetra kṣemakaraḥ pūjyaḥ tad paśvāt vighna nāyakaḥ virūpākṣaḥ nikumbha īśāt vahnau pūjyaḥ su siddhi daḥ tad udīcyām mahā liṅgam devayānīśvarā abhidham yat jalam śraddhayā pītam liṅga trayam arpayet tat ambuprāśanam iti pūrveṇa eva anvayaḥ bhavān īśau namasyau ca śukreśāt paścime śubhau alarkeśaḥ samabhyarcyaḥ śukreśāt pūrva diś sthitaḥ gaṇeśvara īśvaram liṅgam sarva siddhi karam param hatvā laṅkā īśvaram vipraiḥ raghunātha pratiṣṭhitam tad liṅga sparśanāt āśu brahmā api mahā puṇya pradam ca anyat tatra āryam tripurāntakam dattātreya īśvaram liṅgam tasya paścimatas śubham tad yāmyām harikeśa īśaḥ gokarṇa īśaḥ tatas param tad agre dhruva kuṇḍam ca pitṛ prīti karam param raghunā raghu vaṃśa udbhavena rāma ākhyena viṣṇunā iti yāvat tat uktam āraṇyake parvaṇi jātaḥ daśarathasya āsīt rāmaḥ nāma mahātmanaḥ viṣṇuḥ svena śarīreṇa rāvaṇasya vadhāya ca raghunātha iti pāṭhe spaṣṭaḥ eva arthaḥ tad uttare piśāca īśaḥ paiśācya pada hārakaḥ pitrīśaḥ tad yama diśi pitṛkuṇḍam tad agratas tatra śrāddha kṛtām puṃsām tuṣyeyuḥ prapitāmahāḥ agre dhruva īśāt tāra īśaḥ vaidya nāthaḥ saḥ eva hi tat nairṛtyām manoḥ liṅgam vaṃśa vṛddhi karam param tad yāmyām mucukunda īśaḥ tad pārśve gautameśvaraḥ tad paścime tu bhadreśaḥ tad yāmyām ṛṣya śṛṅgiṇaḥ tad prācyām nahuṣa īśaḥ ca viśālākṣī ca tad puras viśālākṣīśvaram liṅgam tatra eva kṣetra vasti dam marāsaṃdheśvaram liṅgam tat yāmyām jvara nāśanam tat purastāt hiraṇyākṣa liṅgam pūjyam hiraṇya dam tad paścime gayā adhīśaḥ taṭha pratīcyām bhagīrathaḥ tatra liṅgam sa kuṇḍam ca snātuḥ iṣṭa phala pradam tatra viśvāvasoḥ liṅgam muṇḍeśaḥ tatra pūrvatas tad dakṣiṇe vidhīśaḥ ca tad yāmyām vājimedhakaḥ daśāśvamedhike snātvā dṛṣṭvā tat liṅgam uttamam daśānām aśvamedhānām phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ tad uttare mātṛtīrtham snātuḥ janma bhaya apahṛt tatra snānam tu yaḥ kuryāt nārī vā puruṣaḥ api vā īpsitam phalam āpnoti mātṝṇām ca prasādāt tava kuṇḍāt ca puṣpadanteśvaraḥ paraḥ tad agni diśi devarṣi gaṇa liṅgāni anekaśas puṣpadantāt dakṣiṇatas siddhīśaḥ para siddhi daḥ pañca upacāra pūjāyāḥ svapne siddhim parām diśet rājya prāptiḥ bhavet puṃsām hariścandra īśa sevayā tad dakṣiṇe ca kṣemeśaḥ citrāṅga īśaḥ tatas yame tad dakṣiṇe ca kedāraḥ rudra anucara tā pradaḥ candra sūrya anvayaiḥ bhūpaiḥ kedārāt dakṣiṇāpathe pratiṣṭhitāni liṅgāni śataśas atha sahasraśas lola arkāt dakṣiṇa āśāyām sarva āśāpūrakaḥ arcitaḥ harandhameśvaram liṅgam taṭhapratīcyām mahā phalam tad paścime mahādurgā mahā durga prabhañjanā ca manakeśaḥ taṭha pratīcyām śaṅkukarṇaḥ tad uttare mahā siddhīśvaram liṅgam tatyācyām sarva siddhi dam siddhakuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā siddheśvaram mahat sarvāsām eva siddhīnām pāram gacchati mānavaḥ maṅkukarṇa īśa vāyavye liṅgam vāyavya saṃjñitam sarva āśāpūrakaḥ arkavināyakaḥ iti śeṣaḥ śuṣkayā asīnāmnyā nadyā tad agre ca vibhāṇḍa īśaḥ kahola īśaḥ tad uttare tatra dvāreśvaram liṅgam devī dvāreśvarī śubhā rakṣakāḥ ca gaṇāḥ tatra nānā rūpa āyudhāḥ mune tatra eva haridīśam ca liṅgam kātyāyanam tatas tad pārśve jāṅgaleśaḥ ca tad paścāt mukuṭeśvaraḥ snātvā mukuṭa kuṇḍe ca dṛṣṭvā vai mukuṭeśvaram yātrayā sarva liṅgānām yat phalam tat avāpyate tapasaḥ ca api yogasya siddhi dā sā avanī parā mune śatam sahasrāṇi tatra liṅgāni siddhaye ekā diś uttarā devi vārāṇasyām priyā mama satyam satyam punar satyam tri satyam na anyatas priye uddeśa mātram liṅgāni kathitāni mayā mune sthāpitāni bhaktyā liṅgāni kānicid etāni yāni liṅgāni yāni kuṇḍāni ye andhavaḥ yāḥ vā apyaḥ tāni sarvāṇi śraddheyāni manīṣibhiḥ eteṣām darśanāt snānāt phalam atra uttarottaram atratyānām ca liṅgānām kūpānām sarasām api ca api saṃkhyātum prabhuḥ bhavet mad ānanda kānana sthāni tṛṇāni api param varam sarva liṅga mayā kāśā sarva tīrtha eka janma bhūḥ svarga apavargayoḥ dātrī dṛṣṭā dehānta sevitā svabhāvāt tu iyam kāśā sukha viśrāma bhūḥ mama ye kāśyāḥ nāma gṛhṇanti ye anumodante eva hi te me śākhā viśākhā ābhāḥ skanda nandi gaja āsya vat taiḥ ca dattam mahā dānam ye ca ānanda vanaukasaḥ te snāta sarva tīrthāḥ vai te akhila adhvara dīkṣitāḥ akhilāḥ antyajaḥ api varaḥ kāśyām na anyatra śruti pāragaḥ saṃsāra pāragaḥ pūrvaḥ tu antyaśvā antyajaḥ api adhas saḥ eva nūnam sarvajñaḥ saḥ eva hi adhika īkṣaṇaḥ yaḥ pārthivām tanum hitvā kāśyām dhatte sudhā mayām bhāga śrutvā adhyāyam idam puṇyam puṇyam sarva tīrtha rahasyavat prāpnoti yaḥ paṭhet imam adhyāyam prātar prātar dine dine dṛṣṭāni tena sarvāṇi tīrthāni etāni na anyathā sarva liṅga mayā adhyāyam yaḥ amum nityam japet sudhīḥ na tam yamaḥ na tam dūtāḥ na enam aṃhaḥ api bādhate brahmayajña phalam tasya jāyate sukṛta ātmanaḥ sa snātaḥ sarva kuṇḍeṣu sarva vāpī ambupaḥ sa ca sakṛt japāt mahā adhyāyāt amuṣmāt tat samāpyate śrutvā adhyāyam idam puṇyam iti idam puṇyam ākhyānam śrutvā tat adhyāya snātvā sarvāṇi tīrthāni dṛṣṭvā liṅgāni anekaśas tad kāśi liṅgāvalī nāmā adhyāyaḥ japyeta yat mune ca api tathā abhakṣyasya bhakṣaṇam mātā pitṛ vadhāt jātam go bhrūṇa hanana udbhavam mahā pāpāni pāpāni jñāta ajñātāni bhūriśas upapāpāni pāpāni manas vāc kāya jāni api yānti putrān pautrān dhanam dhānyam kalatram kṣetram eva ca manaḥ samīhitam sarvam svargam mokṣam sukhāni api japtvā adhyāyam imam vidvāḥ prāpsyati eva na saṃśayaḥ iti śrī rāmānanda kṛtāyām kāśīkhaṇḍa ṭīkāyām saptanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ iti yāvat samākhyāti devaḥ devī puras kathām jātā parisamāptiḥ ca mahā prāsāda nirmiteḥ sajjīkṛtaḥ rathaḥ ca ayam brahma ādyāḥ militāḥ surāḥ tārkṣya gaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ dvāri tiṣṭhati sa anugaḥ pratīkṣamāṇaḥ avasaram puraskṛtya muni īśvarān caturdaśasu lokeṣu ye ye tiṣṭhanti suvratāḥ te niśamya adya militāḥ prāveśika mahā utsavam iti nandi vacaḥ śrutvā devaḥ devī samāyutaḥ divyam ratham samāruhya nirjagāma triviṣṭapāt iti śrī skandapurāṇe kāśīkhaṇḍe kṣetratīrthavarṇanam nāma saptanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha aṣṭanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca śṛṇu sūta mahābhāga yathā skandena bhāṣitaḥ niśāmaya mahā prājña śambhuprāveśikīm kathām trailokya ānanda jananīm mahāpātaka taṅkinīm mandarāt āgataḥ śambhuḥ caitre damanaparvaṇi prāpya api ānanda gahanam itas ca itas cacāra ha aṣṭa adhike navati ākhye adhyāye tāvat nirucyate śrī muktimaṇḍape śrīmat viśveśvara samāgamaḥ nāśinīm damanaparvaṇi damana trayodaśyām caitra śukla trayodaśyām iti arthaḥ prāpyā api iti mokṣa lakṣmīvilāse atha prāsāde siddhim āgate devaḥ virajasaḥ pīṭhāt antar geham viveśa ha candre saptama rāśi sthe śeṣeṣu ucca graheṣu ca vādyamāneṣu vādyeṣu prasannāsu haritsu ca brāhmaṇānām śruti rava nyakkṛta anya rava antare sarvam pramuditam ca āsīt śambhoḥ prāveśika utsave ha jaguḥ gandharva nikarāḥ nanṛtuḥ ca apsaras gaṇāḥ cāraṇāḥ tu stutim kuryuḥ jahṛṣuḥ devatā gaṇāḥ virajasaḥ pīṭhāt trilocanam sthānāt vavuḥ gandha vahāḥ vātāḥ vavṛṣuḥ kusumaiḥ ghanāḥ sarve maṅgala nepathyāḥ sarve maṅgala bhāṣiṇaḥ sthāvarāḥ jaṅgamāḥ sarve jātāḥ ānanda medurāḥ sura asureṣu sarveṣu gandharveṣu urageṣu ca ca strī puṃs jāteṣu sarveṣu rejuḥ catvāraḥ rejuḥ catvāraḥ eva ca niṣpratyūham ca nitarām puruṣa arthāḥ pade pade nīrājanāya ye dīpāḥ tadā sarve prabodhitāḥ teṣām jyotīṃṣi khe adya api rājante tāraka ācchalāt pratisaudham patākāḥ ca nānā ākārāḥ vicitritāḥ kvacid gāyanti gīta jñāḥ kvacid nṛtyanti nartakāḥ harita śveta māñjiṣṭha nīla pīta bahu prabhāḥ prati aṅgaṇam śubha ākārāḥ raṅga mālāḥ cakāśire ratna kuṭṭima bhūbhāgāḥ gopura agreṣu rejire yāni kāni iha kīrtyante maṅgalāni ghaṭodbhavaiḥ teṣām eva hi sarveṣām tat tu janma divā abhavat maṭāḥ prakṣepāḥ bindavaḥ vā raṅga mālāḥ utsava nimittaka mālāḥ atha a bhiṣiktaḥ caturānanena mahā ṛṣi vṛndaiḥ saha devadevaḥ śubha āsana sthaḥ sahitaḥ bhavānyā kumāra vṛndaiḥ paritas ghṛtaḥ ca apūpujan deva gaṇāḥ maheśam tadā mudā te ca mahā uraga indrāḥ sampūjitaḥ kumbhajaiḥ tatra śambhuḥ nīrājitaḥ mātṛ gaṇaiḥ atha īṃśaḥ santoṣya sarvān prathamam muni indrān svaiḥ svaiḥ hṛdisthaiḥ ca cira abhilāṣaiḥ brahmānam ābhāṣya śivaḥ atha viṣṇum jagāda sarva amara vṛnda vanyaḥ tvayā divodāsa narendra varyaḥ sat upadeśaiḥ ca tathā upadiṣṭaḥ kumāra vṛndāḥ gaṇeśa kārttikeya samūhāḥ sanaka ādayaḥ vā idam mayā ānanda vanam yat āptam hetuḥ tu tatra tvam asau gaṇeśaḥ vārāṇasī brahma rasāyanasya khaniḥ janiḥ yatra na dīrghaśāyinām śrutvā iti vākyam jagadīśituḥ ca provāca viṣṇuḥ vara dam maheśam yadi prasannaḥ asi pinākapāṇe tadā pada adūram aham na te syām śrutvā iti vākyam madhusūdanasya jagāda tuṣṭaḥ nitarām purāriḥ sadā murāre mama saṃnidhau tvam tiṣṭhasva nirvāṇa ramā āśraye atra dīrgha śāyinām tyakta prāṇānām lakṣmīpati mokṣa lakṣmyāḥ sadmani sthātum ucitam iti bhāvaḥ nimeṣa mātram sthira citta vṛttayaḥ tiṣṭhanti ye dakṣiṇa maṇḍape atra mama ananya bhāvāḥ api gāḍha mānasāḥ na te punar garbha daśām upāsate te mama pārṣadāḥ hi śṛṇvanti puṇyāḥ ca kathāḥ kṣaṇam sthirāḥ te koṭi go dāna phalam bhajanti upendra taptāni tapāṃsi taiḥ ciram snātāḥ hi te ca akhila tīrtha sārthakaiḥ snātvā iha ye vai maṇi karṇikā hade samāsate mukti janāśraye kṣaṇam tīrthāni santi iha pade pade hare tulā kva teṣām maṇikarṇikāyāḥ kati iha no santi śubhāḥ ca maṇḍapāḥ param paraḥ mukti ramā āśrayaḥ ayam niścala śriyi niścalā śrīḥ yasmin tasmin loke khyātiḥ bhavitrī iyam eṣa kukkuṭa maṇḍapaḥ bhāla netra samākhyāhi katham nirvāṇa maṇḍapaḥ tathā khyātim asau gantā yathā devena bhāṣitam tat sadā eva atithi vallabhaḥ viṣama iṣu śaraiḥ tītraiḥ kāritaḥ tu apade padam maitrīm kṛtvā tu tena vai ṛgvedī vaiṣṇavān dhaninaḥ dṛṣṭvā kṣaṇam vaiṣṇava veṣa bhṛt hi śaivān nindati mūḍha ātmā naraka trāṇa kāraṇam iti pākhaṇḍa dharma jñaḥ sandhyā snāna parāṅmukhaḥ viśāla tilakaḥ sragvī śuddha dhauta ambara ujjvalaḥ mama asmi dhanī ditsuḥ jātyā cāṇḍāla sattamaḥ iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā kaiścid ca aṅguli saṃjñayā aṣṭanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uddiṣṭaḥ upaviṣṭaḥ asau yaḥ japet dhyāna mudrayā iti teṣām vacaḥ śrutvā sa gatvā tad samīpatas daṇḍa vāṇi patyā atha tam babhāṣe tadā antyajaḥ mama tattvam gṛhāṇa anugraham kuru atha akṣamālikām karṇe kṛtvā dhyānam visṛjya ca tava asti iha papraccha karaṃ saṃjñayā tat ca saṃjñām sa vai buddhvā provāca ati prahṛṣṭa vat sat tṛptiḥ yāvatā te syāt tāvat dāsyāmi na a anyathā na stokam api dātavyam tadā ādāsyāmi na anyathā uvāca asti tāvat te pradāsyāmi viśveśaḥ tvam yatas mama ye vasanti iha viśveśa rājadhānyām dvijottamaiḥ kṣudrā kṣudrā jantu mātrā viśveśa aṃśāḥ te eva hi para uddharaṇa śīlāḥ ye ye para icchā prapūrakāḥ para upakṛti śīlāḥ ye viśveśa aṃśāḥ te eva hi iti tad vacanam tad vacanam śrutvā śrutvā prahṛṣṭa indriya mānasaḥ uvāca pārvatīyam tam saḥ agrajanmā antyajam tadā ādāsyāmi iti chedaḥ māyāhi darbhān ā ādehi kuru utsargam tvarā anvitaḥ tathā iti saḥ cakāra āśu pārvatīyaḥ mahāmanāḥ viśveśaḥ prīyatām ca iti procya yātaḥ yathā āgataḥ cāṇḍāla brāhmaṇaḥ ca eṣa cāṇḍāla ātta dhanaḥ tu asau asau eva hi cāṇḍālaḥ sarva loka bahiṣkṛtaḥ saḥ ekadā sampradhārya gṛhiṇyā loka dūṣitaḥ jagāma kīkaṭān deśān tyaktvā vārāṇasīm purīm pārvatīyaḥ yātaḥ sva deśam gataḥ tiraskṛtaḥ tad pāde akṣara ādhikyam ārṣam nītvā te tam araṇyānīm taskarāḥ sa paricchadam tvām vayam ghātayiṣyāmaḥ niścitam sa paricchadam aho pratigṛhītam mama yad artham vasu bhūriśas tat naṣṭam naṣṭaḥ ca api pratigrahaḥ mama naṣṭam naṣṭā kāśi purī sthitiḥ tān kīkaṭān gayā pradeśān sa kāñcanaḥ svarṇavān yugapad sarvam eva āśu naṣṭam durbuddhi ceṣṭayā na kāśau maraṇam prāptam tasmāt duṣṭa pratigrahāt prānte kuṭumba smaraṇāt tathā kāśi smṛtyāḥ api sā kukkuṭī sutau tau tu tāmracūḍa tvam āpatuḥ prānte kāśi smaraṇāt jātā jāti smṛtiḥ parā ittham bahutithe kāle gate kārpaṭika uttamāḥ tasmin eva adhvani prāptāḥ catvāraḥ yatra kukkuṭāḥ proccais kurvantaḥ anyonyam eva hi kāśi kathām samākarṇya tadā te caraṇa āyudhāḥ jāti smṛti prabhāvena tad saṅgena tu nirgatāḥ taiḥ ca kārpaṭika śreṣṭhaiḥ pathini dṛṣṭvā kṛpālubhiḥ taṇḍula ādi parikṣepaiḥ prāpitāḥ kṣetram uttamam te tu kṣetram samāsādya catvāraḥ caraṇa āyudhāḥ jita āhārān sa niyamān kāma krodha parāṅmukhān mad kathā ālāpān lobha moha vivarjitān mad nāma uccāraṇa parān mad kathā arpita suśrutīn mad datta citta sat vṛttīn dṛṣṭvā kṣetra nivāsinaḥ mānayāmāsuḥ atha tān kukkuṭān sādhu vartmanaḥ prāṇān tyakṣyanti ca atra vai cariṣyantaḥ cariṣyanti paryaṭiṣyanti iti arthaḥ jita āhārān iti ādeḥ mānayāmāsuḥ atha iti paśyatām sarva lokānām viṣṇo te mad anugrahāt padam mayā dṛśyatām iti śloka dvayam vākyam he viṣṇo te catvāraḥ kukkuṭāḥ iti anuṣajjate mad padam prāpya bhogān nirviśya bhuktvā atra kāśau kailāse vā jñāninaḥ bhūtvā tena eva śarīreṇa iti śeṣaḥ śāśvatām muktim prāpsyanti iti anvayaḥ nanu tatra āha mad anugrahāt iti antakāle kāśi smaraṇāt mad toṣaṇāt jātaḥ yaḥ mad anugrahaḥ ete bhukti muktī mayā prāpaṇīyā nirviśya su ciram kālam divyān bhogān anuttamān tatas atra jñāninaḥ bhūtvā muktim prāpsyanti śāśvatām muktimaṇḍapa nām etat eṣa kukkuṭa maṇḍapaḥ caritram api vai teṣām ye smariṣyanti mānavāḥ mukti maṇḍapam āsādya śreyaḥ prāpsyanti te api hi iti yāvat kathām śambhuḥ bhaviṣyām agratas hareḥ tumulaḥ nādaḥ ghaṇṭānām tāvat udgataḥ provāca nandin vijñāya āgatya brūhi kutas ravaḥ namaskṛtya prahṛṣṭa āsyaḥ prabaddha kara sampuṭaḥ tumulaḥ nādaḥ iti liṅga rūpiṇaḥ viśveśasya dhruvam vidārya udbhūtaḥ ghaṇṭānām iva nādaḥ jāta utthāya devadeveśaḥ saha devyā sumaṅgalaḥ brahmanā hariṇā sārdham tatas agāt raṅga maṇḍapam ca adhyāyam imam puṇyam parama ānanda kāraṇam naraḥ parām mudam prāpya kailāsam prāpsyati dhruvam iti śrī skandapurāṇe kāśīkhaṇḍe muktimaṇḍapagamanam nāma aṣṭanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ mokṣa lakṣmī vilāsaḥ mokṣa lakṣmyāḥ vilāsaḥ syām adṛśyaḥ syām kadācana mad ānanda kānane ca atra svairam tiṣṭhāmi devatāḥ anugrahāya sarveṣām bhaktānām iha sarvadā sthāsyāmi liṅga rūpeṇa cintita artha phala pradaḥ yāni yāni liṅgāni sarvatas adhyāyaḥ uvāca idam skāndam aham śrutvā kāśīkhaṇḍam anuttamam nitarām paritṛptaḥ asmi hṛdi ca api vidhāritam tathā māhātmyam uttamam pārāśarya samācakṣva yathāpūrvam idam bhavet niśāmaya śuka vaiśampāyana ādyāḥ śṛṇvantu api ca bālakāḥ anukramaṇikā adhyāyam māhātmyam ca api khaṇḍa jam tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat atha adhyāye śatatame sarva abhīṣṭa phala prade pūrva adhyāya ante idānīm praṣṭu kāmaḥ asi kim tat pṛccha vadāmi te iti uktam tatra uktā anuvāda pūrvakam tṛptim āviṣkurvan anukramaṇikā tad māhātmye pṛcchati idam skānda māhātmye satya loka prabhāvaḥ ca dvitīyaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ agasteḥ āśrama pade devānām āgamaḥ tatas tīrtha praśaṃsā ca tatas sapta paryastāt smṛtāḥ indra agnyoḥ loka samprāptiḥ tatas ca śivaśarmaṇaḥ tad prathama adhyāya artham āha vindhya iti dvitīya adhyāya artham āha satya iti tṛtīya adhyāya artham āha agasteḥ iti caturtha adhyāya artham āha pativratā iti tasmāt tatas śukra samudbhavaḥ māheya guru saurīṇām lokānām varṇanam tatas saptarṣīṇām tatas lokāḥ dhruvasya ca tapaḥ tatas darśanam satya lokasya tasya vai śivaśarmaṇaḥ caturbhujā abhiṣekaḥ ca nirvāṇam śivaśarmaṇaḥ skanda agastyoḥ ca saṃvādaḥ maṇikarṇyāḥ samudbhavaḥ tatas tu gaṅgāmāhātmyam tatas daśa hara āstavaḥ prabhāvaḥ ca api gaṅgāyāḥ gaṅgā nāma sahasrakam vārāṇasyāḥ praśaṃsā atha bhairava āvirbhavaḥ tatas pañcadaśā adhyāya artham āha iti tasmāt tad anantaram uḍuloka kathā iti anvayaḥ tamaḥ adhyāyaḥ daṇḍapāṇeḥ samudbhūtiḥ jñāna vāpī uddhavaḥ tatas mad brahmacāri prakaraṇam tatas strī lakṣaṇāni ca tyā akṛtya prakaraṇam avimukta īśa varṇanam tatas kāla jñānam tatas proktam divodāsasya varṇanam tasmāt yoginī varṇanam tatas lola arkasya samākhyānam uttara arka kathā tatas dvātriṃśat adhyāya artham āha daṇḍapāṇeḥ iti trayastriṃśat adhyāya artham āha jñāna vāpī iti catur triṃśat adhyāya artham āha ākhyānam ca iti pañcatriṃśat adhyāya artham āha sat ācāraḥ iti ṣaṭtriṃśat adhyāya artham āha iti saptatriṃśat adhyāya artham āha tatas strī iti triṃśat adhyāya artham āha kṛtyā akṛtyā iti ekonacatvāriṃśat adhyāya artham āha avimukte sāmba ādityasya mahimā drupada āditya śaṃsanam tatas tu garuḍa ākhyānam aruṇa arka ādayaḥ tatas daśāśvamedhikam tīrtham mandarāt ca gaṇāgamaḥ piśāca mocana ākhyānam gaṇeśa preṣaṇam tatas māyā gaṇa pateḥ ca atha duṇḍi prādurbhavaḥ tatas tatas vaiṣṇava tīrthānām māhātmya parivarṇanam prayāṇam mandarāt kāśīm vṛṣabhadhvaja śūlinaḥ jaigīṣavyena saṃvādaḥ jyeṣṭhasthāne maheśituḥ tad aṣṭacatvāriṃśat adhyāya artham āha sāmba ādityasya iti ekonapañcāśat adhyāya artham āha tatas kṣetra rahasyasya kathanam pāpa nāśanam tatas śaileśvara kathā ratneśasya caṃ darśanam tatas kṛttivāsaḥ samutpattiḥ tatas ca āyatana āgamaḥ devatānām adhiṣṭhānam durgā asura parākramaḥ durgāyāḥ vijayaḥ ca atha tatas oṃkāra varṇanam punar oṃkāra māhātmyam trilocana samudbhavaḥ tatas dharmeśa mahimā tatas pakṣi kathā śubhā catuḥṣaṣṭi adhyāya artham āha tatas kṣetra iti pañcaṣaṣṭi adhyāya artham āha atha atas iti tathaśabdaḥ atra liṅga prādurbhāve maṅgala arthaḥ ṣaṭṣaṣṭi adhyāya artham āha tatas śaileśvara iti saptaṣaṣṭi adhyāya artham āha iti tatas ca āyata iti ekonasaptati adhyāya artham āha tatas ca āyata tatas vīra īśvara ākhyānam vīra īśa mahimā punar gaṅgā tīrthaiḥ ca saṃyuktā kāmeśa mahimā tatas dakṣa yajña samudbhavaḥ satī īśvara samutpattiḥ amṛta īśa ādi varṇanam tīrtha kadambam ca mukti maṇḍapa saṃkathā etat ākhyānaśatakam krameṇa parikīrtitam yasya śravaṇa mātreṇa sarva khaṇḍa śrutyāḥ phalam tatra anukramaṇikā adhyāye api asti yātrā parikramaḥ dvyaśīti adhyāya artham āha tatas vīra iti tryaśīti adhyāya artham āha vīra īśa iti caturaśīti adhyāya artham āha aśīti adhyāya artham āha gaṅgā iti pañcāśīti adhyāya artham āha kāmeśa iti ṣaḍaśīti adhyāya artham āha viśvakarmā iti saptāśīti adhyāya artham āha dakṣa yajña iti aṣṭāśīti adhyāya artham āha satyāḥ iti navāśīti adhyāya artham āha tatas dakṣa iti pañcanavati adhyāya artham āha iti ṣaṇṇavati adhyāya artham āha vyāsa śāpa iti saptanavati adhyāya artham āha kṣetra iti aṣṭanavati adhyāya artham āha mukti maṇḍapa iti taḥ uvāca yātrā parikramam brūhi janānām hita kāmyayā yathāvat siddhi kāmānām satyavatyāḥ suta uttamaiḥ niśāmaya mahā prājña lomaharṣaṇa vacmi te sa cailam ādau saṃsnāya cakra puṣkariṇī jale santarpya devān sa pitṝn brāhmaṇān ca tathā arthinaḥ maheśvaram namaskṛtya tatas gacchet draṣṭum duṇḍi vināyakam navanavati adhyāya artham āha viśveśa iti śatatama adhyāya artham āha tatas yātrā iti tārakeśam tatas abhyarcya mahākāla īśvaram tatas tatas punar daṇḍapāṇim iti eṣā pañca tīrthikā tatas vaiśveśvarī yātrā kāryā sarva artha siddhi dā dvisapta āyatanānām ca kāryā yātrā prayatnāt kṛṣṇām pratipadam prāpya bhūta avadhi yathāvidhi tad tad tīrtha kṛta snānaḥ tad tad liṅga kṛta arcanaḥ maunena yātrām kurvāṇaḥ phalam prāpnoti yātrikaḥ oṃkāram prathamam paśyet matsya udarāyām kṛta udakaḥ triviṣṭapam mahādevam tatas vai kṛttivāsasam ratneśam ca atha candreśam kedāram ca tatas vrajet bhāva vāpīm iti śloka uktam caturtham tatas iti pāda uktam pañcamam iti eṣā pañcatīrthikā iti pūrva ukta rūpā vā dharmeśvaram ca vīreśam gacchet kāmeśvaram tatas viśvakarmeśvaram ca atha maṇikarṇīśvaram tatas avimukteśvaram dṛṣṭvā tatas viśveśam arcayet eṣā yātrā prayatnena kartavyā kṣetra vāsinā yaḥ tu kṣetram uṣitvā tu na etām yātrām samācaret vighnāḥ tasya upatiṣṭhante kṣetra uccāṭana sūcakāḥ tri āyatana yātrā anyā kartavyā vighna śāntaye dakṣeśaḥ pārvatīśaḥ ca tathā paśupatīśvaraḥ aṣṭamaḥ tāraka īśaḥ ca pratyaṣṭame viśeṣataḥ dṛśyāni etāni liṅgāni mahā pāpa upaśāntaye aparā api śubhā yātrā yogakṣema karā sadā mahā īśam prathamam vīkṣya varaṇā snāna pūrvakam snānam tu saṃgame kṛtvā draṣṭavyaḥ saṃgameśvaraḥ sva līna tīrthe su snātaḥ paśyet sva līnam īśvaram snātvā mandākinītīrthe draṣṭavyaḥ madhyameśvaraḥ paśyet hiraṇyagarbha īśam tatra tīrthe kṛta udakaḥ tatas snātvā paśyet īśānam īśvaram kāpileyahade snātvā vīkṣeta vṛṣabhadhvajam upaśānta śivam paśyet tad kūpa vihita udakaḥ pañcacūḍā hade snātvā jyeṣṭhasthānam tatas arcayet devasya agre tu yā vāpī tatra upasparśane kṛte hi śukreśvaram tatas paśyet tad kūpa vihita udakaḥ daṇḍakhāte tatas snātvā vyāghra īśam pūjayet tatas haunakeśvara kuṇḍe tu snānam kṛtvā tatas arcayet mahā liṅgam kṛtvā yātrām imām naraḥ kvacid na jāyate bhūyas saṃsāre duḥkha sāgare samārabhya pratipadam yāvat kṛṣṇā caturdaśī imām yātrām naraḥ kṛtvā na bhūyas api abhijāyate anyā yātrā prakartavyā ekādaśa āyatana udbhavā āgnīdhra kuṇḍe su snātaḥ paśyet āgnīdhram īśvaram urvaśīśam tatas gacchet tatas tu nakulīśvaram māṣāḍhīśam tatas dṛṣṭvā bhāra bhūta īśvaram tatas tatas tu tripurāntakam tatas manaḥprakāma īśam prītikeśam atho vrajet madālaseśvaram tasmāt tilaparṇeśvaram tatas yātrā ekādaśa liṅgānām eṣā kāryā prayatnāt imām yātrām prakurvāṇaḥ rudra tvam prāpnuyāt naraḥ antar param pravakṣyāmi gaurīyātrām anuttamān śukla pakṣe tṛtīyāyām yā yātrā viṣvañc ṛddhi dā asau ca asau kramaḥ ca iti etad āyatanāni pūrva ukta śaileśa ādi āśritāni viṣvak ṛddhi dā sarva sampatti dātrī jyeṣṭhāvāpyām naraḥ snātvā jyeṣṭhām gaurīm samarcayet saubhāgyagaurī sampūjyā jñāna vāpyām kṛta udakaiḥ tatas śṛṅgāragaurīm ca tatra eva ca kṛta udakaḥ snātvā viśālagaṅgāyām viśālākṣīm tatas vrajet snātvā bhavānītīrthe atha bhavānīm paripūjayet tatas gacchet mahālakṣmīm sthira lakṣmī samṛddhaye imām yātrām naraḥ kṛtvā kṣetre asmin mukti janmani kuryāt prati caturthī iha yātrām vighneśituḥ sadā brāhmaṇebhyaḥ tad uddeśāt deyāḥ vai modakāḥ modakāḥ mude bhaume bhairavayātrā ca kāryā pātaka hāriṇī ravivāre raveḥ yātrā ṣaṣṭhyām vā ravi saṃyuji navamyām athavā aṣṭamyām caṇḍī yātrā śubhā matā prātar snānam vidhāya ādau natvā pañca vināyakān namaskṛtvā atha viśveśam sthitvā nirvāṇa maṇḍape antargṛhasya yātrām vai kariṣye agha ogha śāntaye gṛhītvā niyamam ca iti gatvā atha maṇikarṇikām snātvā maunena ca āgatya maṇikarṇīśam arcayet kambala aśvatarau natvā vāsukīśam praṇamya ca parvata īśam tatas dṛṣṭvā gaṅgā keśavam api atha tatas tu lalitām dṛṣṭvā jarāsaṃdha īśvaram tatas brahmeśvaram tatas natvā natvā agastīśvaram tatas kaśyapa īśam namaskṛtya namaskṛtya hari keśa vanam hari keśa vanam tatas tatas dṛṣṭvā dhruva īśam atha vīkṣya ca taḍāge ca dṛṣṭvā vai kīkaseśvaram bhāra bhūtam tatas natvā citragupta īśvaram tatas citraghaṇṭām praṇamya atha tatas paśupati īśvaram pitāmaheśvaram gatvā tatas tu kalaśeśvaram candreśaḥ tu atha vīreśaḥ vidyeśaḥ agnīśaḥ eva ca nāgeśvarī hariścandraḥ cintāmaṇi vināyakaḥ senāvināyakaḥ ca atha dravṭavyaḥ sarva vighna hṛt vasiṣṭha vāmadevau ca mūrti rūpa dharau ubhau draṣṭavyau yatnatas kāśau mahā vighna vināśinaḥ sīmā vināyakam ca atha karuṇeśam tatas vrajet trisandhyeśaḥ viśālākṣī dharmeśaḥ viśvabāhukā mahāvināyakaḥ ca atha vṛddhādityaḥ tatas punar caturvaktra īśvaram liṅgam brāhmīśaḥ tu tatas paras tatas manas prakāma īśaḥ īśāna īśaḥ tatas param caṇḍī caṇḍeśvarau dṛśyau bhavānī śaṃkarau tatas duṣṭim praṇamya ca tatas rājarāja īśam arcayet lāṅgalīśaḥ tatas abhyarcyaḥ tatas tu nakuli īśvaraḥ tatas parānna īśam atho natvā paradravyeśvaram tatas pratigraheśvaram vā api niṣkalaṅkeśam eva ca gaṅgeśaḥ abhyarcyaḥ tatas jñāna vāpyām snānam samācaret nandikeśam tārakeśam mahākāleśvaram tatas daṇḍapāṇim maheśam ca mokṣeśam praṇamet tatas natvā tatas pañca viśvanātham tatas vrajet antargṛhasya yātrā iyam yathāvat yā mayā kṛtā nyūna atiriktayā śambhuḥ prīyatām anayā vibhuḥ iti mantram samuccārya kṣaṇam vai mukti maṇḍape viśramya yāyāt bhavanam niṣpāpaḥ puṇyavān naraḥ samprāpya vāsaram viṣṇoḥ viṣṇutīrtheṣu sarvatas kāryā yātrā prayatnena mahā puṇya samṛddhaye duḥkham rudra piśāca tvam na bhavet yasya pūjanāt śraddhā pūrvam imāḥ yātrāḥ kartavyāḥ kṣetra vāsibhiḥ parvasu api viśeṣeṇa kāryāḥ yātrāḥ ca sarvatas na vandhyam divasam kuryāt vinā yātrām kvacid kṛtī yasya vandhyam dinam yātam kāśau nivasataḥ sataḥ saḥ daṣṭaḥ kālasarpeṇa saḥ dṛṣṭaḥ mṛtyunā sphuṭam sa muṣṭaḥ tatra divase viśveśaḥ yatra na īkṣitaḥ maṇikartyām tu yaḥ snātaḥ yaḥ viśveśam niraikṣata satyam satyam punar satyam satyam satyam punar punar dṛśyaḥ viśveśvaraḥ nityam snātavyā maṇikarṇikā uvāca sūtaiḥ skāndam idam śrutvā kāśīmāhātmyam uttamam snātvā sarvāṇi tīrthāni yat śreyaḥ samupārjyate bāśīkhaṇḍasya śravaṇāt tat syāt sūtaiḥ na saṃśayaḥ da tvā dānāni sarvāṇi kṛtvā yajñān anekaśas mad labhate na adhītya caturaḥ vedān sa aṅgān yat phalam āpyate tat phalam labhyate naraiḥ gayāyām śrāddha dānāt ca yathā tṛpyanti pūrvajāḥ tathā etad śravaṇāt nṛṇām tṛpnuvanti pitāmahāḥ taiḥ ca sarva purāṇāni śrutāni sthira buddhibhiḥ tat kāśīkhaṇḍam śrutam yaiḥ ca sarveṣām śreyasām padam sarva dharmāḥ taiḥ mahā puṇya eka rāśibhiḥ hi śrutam yaiḥ sthira cetobhiḥ kāśīmāhātmyam uttamam japet tat khaṇḍam akhilam śrotavyam śraddhayā dvijāḥ śṛṇuyāt ekam api yaḥ ākhyānam kāśi khaṇḍa jam tena sarvāṇi dharma śāstrāṇi asaṃśayam sarva mad prīṇanti amartyāḥ sarve api brahma viṣṇu śiva ādayaḥ hṛṣṭaḥ sarvaḥ bhavet eva bhūta grāmaḥ caturvidhaḥ mahima śravaṇāt asmāt vārāṇasyāḥ na saṃśayaḥ tu ekam vyākhyānam uttamam tasmin tuṣṭe hi san tuṣṭaḥ viśveśaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ yatra etat paṭhyate khaṇḍam parānanda samāśrayam yaḥ idam śṛṇuyāt vidvāḥ yaḥ ca idam śrāvayet sudhīḥ yaḥ paṭhet api puṇya ātmā te sarve rudra mūrtayaḥ akhilāni purāṇāni tena dattāni na a anyathā atra ākhyānāni yāvanti ślokāḥ yāvantaḥ eva hi tathā padāni yāvanti varṇāḥ yāvantaḥ eva hi yāvanti api ca mātrāṇi yāvatyaḥ pada paṅktayaḥ guṇe sūtrāṇi yāvanti yāvantaḥ paṭa tantavaḥ tāvat yuga sahastrāṇi dātā svarge mahīyate etat dvādaśa kṛtvas yaḥ śṛṇuyāt khaṇḍam uttamam aputraḥ śṛṇuyāt yaḥ tu su snātaḥ śraddhayā anvitaḥ yaḥ yaḥ tam tam sa saḥ sadā śrutyā etat prāpnuyāt kṛtī yaḥ kāśīkhaṇḍam uttamam sa kāśi vāsa puṇyasya bhājanam syāt śiva ājñayā saubhāgyam ca api sarvatra prāpnuyāt nirmala āśayaḥ sarveṣām maṅgalānām ca mahā maṅgalam uttamam iti śrī skandapurāṇe kāśīkhaṇḍe anukramaṇikā nāma śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptam ca idam kāśīkhaṇḍam bhakta icchā upātta dehāya kṛṣṇāya haraye namaḥ nyāye kāṇādavartmani atha ca gurutaraḥ gautamaḥ vā akṣapādaḥ sāṃkhye yaḥ devahūti ātmajaḥ iva hi tathā vāsukiḥ yoga śāstre prāñc kāṇḍe bhaṭṭa tulyaḥ sa jayati paramaḥ śrī surendraḥ guruḥ naḥ mad ante atha purāṇa bhārata vidhau śrī satyavatī ātmajaḥ sāṃkhye śrī kapilaḥ kaṇādaḥ iha yaḥ vaiśeṣike gautamaḥ bhaṭṭa ācārya caturbhujaḥ vijayate prāk kāṇḍa kaumārilaḥ sakośā ca vikośā ca dve ṭīke likhite mayā yatra yasya abhilāṣaḥ syāt sā tena parigṛhyatām āsīt kaśyapa vaṃśa bhūṣaṇa maṇiḥ mānyaḥ tena iyam vihitā hitāya vidvasām ṭīkā budhaiḥ vīkṣyatām kāśau śrī puruṣottamena vidvasā bhaṭṭena śuddha ātmanā tantra adhyātma purāṇa bhārata vida upās upakaṃsāriṇā rāmānanda muni indra varya kṛtayā gūḍha arthayā ṭīkayā samyak saṅkalitam hitāya vidvasām śrī kāśikhaṇḍam mahat mad paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācārya bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣya śrī rāmendravana śiṣyeṇa caitanya tad apara paryāyeṇa rāmānandena kṛtāyām kāśīkhaṇḍa ṭīkāyām śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptā ca iyam kāśīkhaṇḍa ṭīkā kāśīkhaṇḍa punīta yaha karata su maṅgala vṛddhi mahā ānanda saṃskṛta viśva vid
